'PHAGS PAS GZHI DANG ZHES PA'I GZHUNG GI DNGOS BSTAN GYI GZUNG
RTOG DE KUN BYANG SO SOR MA PHYE BAR SPYIR DMIGS, DE YI GNYEN PO

DE RNAM BYANG PHYOGS KYI

CHOS KHO NA LA DMIGS PAS KHYAB PAR BZHED, SLOB DPON NI, GZHI
DANG ZHES PA'I DNGOS BSTAN GYI GZUNG RTOG LA KUN NAS NYON MONGS
PHYOGS KYI CHOS KHO NA LA DMIGS PAS KHYAB, DE YI GNYEN PO YI,
ZHES PA'I DNGOS BSTAN GYI GZUNG RTOG LA RNAM BYANG PHYOGS KYI
CHOS KHO NA LA DMIGS PAS KHYAB PAR BZHED PA'I PHYIR,

PHYI MA DER THAL, GZHI DANG ZHES PA'I DNGOS BSTAN GYI GZUNG RTOG
DANG PO'I DMIGS YUL DU GYUR PA'I RNAM BYANG PHYOGS KYI CHOS MED
PAR BZHED, DE YI GNYEN PO YI, ZHES PA'I DNGOS BSTAN GYI GZUNG
RTOG GI DMIGS YUL DU GYUR PA'I RNAM BYANG PHYOGS KYI CHOS DE,
GZHI DANG ZHES PA'I DNGOS BSTAN GYI GZUNG RTOG

DANG PO'I DMIGS YUL DU GYUR PA'I NYON MONGS PHYOGS KYI CHOS KYI
GNYEN PO'I RIGS SU BZHED PA'I PHYIR, DER THAL, DE YI GNYEN PO
YI, ZHES GSUNGS PA'I PHYIR, RTZA BA'I RTAGS DANG PO MA GRUB NA,
DER THAL, 'PHAGS PA'I LUGS LA, GZHI DANG ZHES PA'I DNGOS BSTAN
GYI GZUNG RTOG DANG PO'I DMIGS YUL DU

GYUR BA'I RNAM BYANG PHYOGS KYI CHOS YOD PA'I PHYIR, DER THAL,
DE'I DMIGS YUL 'CHAD PA'I SKABS SU, MDO LAS, GZUGS NANG STONG PA
NYID DANG DNGOS PO MED PA'I NGO BO NYID STONG PA NYID KYI BAR DU
MI SHES MI MTHONG, ZHES DANG, GZUGS KUN NAS NYON MONGS PAR MI
SHES MI MTHONG, RNAM PAR BYANG BAR MI SHES

MI MTHONG, ZHES DANG, GZUGS GNAS PA MA YIN JI LTAR GNAS PA MA
YIN ZHE NA, SBYIN PA'I PHA ROL TU PHYIN PA LA GNAS PA MA YIN
ZHES GSUNGS PA'I PHYIR, PHYI MA DER THAL, DE YI GNYEN PO YI,
ZHES PA'I DNGOS BSTAN GYI RNAM BYANG GZUNG RTOG LA RNAM BYANG
PHYOGS KYI CHOS KHO NA LA DMIGS PAS KHYAB PAR BSTAN

PAR BZHED PA'I PHYIR, 'PHAGS PAS DE GNYIS KYI DNGOS BSTAN 'GAL
BAR BZHED KYANG, SPYIR SHES SGRIB NYON MONGS GZUNG RTOG DANG
RNAM BYANG GZUNG RTOG 'GAL BAR MA BZHED DE, GZHI DANG ZHES PA'I
DNGOS BSTAN GYI GZUNG RTOG DE RNAM BYANG GZUNG RTOG DANG NYON
MONGS GZUNG RTOG GNYIS KA YIN, NYON MONGS PHYOGS

PA, ,BLO BZANG GRAGS PA'I LUGS BZANG RMAD DU BYUNG, ,DE PHYIR
MGON DE'I BKA' DRIN BSAM MI KHYAB, ,DE BSAB PHYIR DU DON GNYER
'GA' ZHIG LA, ,PHAN PAR SRID SNYAM SPYI DON 'DI BYAS SO, ,DE
PHYIR GZUR GNAS BLO GROS LDAN RNAMS KYIS, ,

RNYED BKUR DON GNYER DRI MAS MA GOS PAR, ,RANG GZHAN DON GNYES
BSGRUB PAR BYA BA'I PHYIR, ,'JUG DGOS 'DI LA THOS BSAM SGOM GSUM
GYIS, ,'JUG PAR RIGS SO BRTZON PAS STOBS BSKYED CIG ,'ON KYANG
BDAG NI BLO DMAN BRTZON PA CHUNG, ,ZAB MO'I LAM 'DI RTAGS PAR
SHIN TU DKA', ,DE'I PHYIR

@140B BDAG BLO KU SHA'I RTZE MO YIS, ,GZHAL NUS MIN YANG CUNG
ZAD 'DIR BKOD LA, ,NONGS PAR MCHIS RNAMS MKHAS PA'I SPYAN SNGAR
BSHAGS, ,DGE 'DIS MTSON PA'I DUS GSUM DANG 'BREL BA'I, ,BDAG
GZHAN DGE BA'I RTZA BA BCI MCHIS PA, ,GNAS SKABS ZAB MO'I DON
'DI LEGS RTOGS NAS, ,MAR

THUG BYANG CHUB CHEN PO MYUR 'THOB SHOG ,DE MA THOB KYI TSE RABS
THAMS CAD DU, ,BLO BZANG BSTAN PA'I RGYAL MTSAN PHYOGS KUN TU,
,BSGRENG LA SA STENG 'GRAN ZLAM MCHIS PA'I, ,PHYOGS LAS RNAM PAR
RGYAL BA 'THOB PAR SHOG ,'DI NYID 'CHAD DANG NYAN PAR BYED PA
RNAMS ,RGYAL BA'I SPYAN SNGAR SKYANG BAR ZHAL BZHES PA,,

ZHING SKYONG GZI LDAN DBANG PHYUG 'KHOR BCAS KYIS, ,G-YAL BA
MED PAR RTAG TU GROGS BYED SHOG ,SHES RAB KYI PHA ROL TU PHYIN
PA'I MAN NGAG GI BSTAN BCOS MNGON PAR RTOGS PA'I RGYAN RTZA
'GRAL GYI SPYI DON RNAM BSHAD SNYING PO RGYAN GYI SNANG BA ZHES
BYA BA, MKHAS SHING GRUB PA BRNYES PA'I DGE SLONG DGE 'DUN BSTAN
PA DAR

RGYAL KYIS MDZAD PA'I SKABS DANG PO'I RNAM BSHAD BSHAD ZIN TO,,
` ,,AOm SVASTI, 'OG MIN GNAS SU NGES PA LNGA LDAN DU, ,MNGON PAR
SANG RGYAS LNGA BDO'I 'GRO 'DREN PHYIR, ;SGYU 'PHRUL LAS BLTAMS
RNAM 'DREN NYI MA'I GNYEN, ,GANG GI GSUNG RAB SHER PHYIN

DGONGS PA'I GNAS, ,SBAS DON JI BZHIN GSAL MDZAD MI PHAM MGON,
,THOG MED SKU MCHED LA SOGS MKHAS RNAMS KYI, ,ZAB RGYAS LEGS
BSHAD RIN CHEN 'BYUNG KHUNG LAS, ,RNAM BSHAD BSAM 'PHEL DBANG GI
RGYAL PO RNYED, ,LUNG RIGS DPYAD GSUM DAG PA'I RNAM DPYOD KYIS,
,THUB BSTAN RGYAL

MTSAN RTZAR BKOD RNAM DKAR MTHUS, ,RGYAL BSTAN SPYI DANG RJE
BTZUN BTZONG KHA PA'I, ,BSHAD SGRUB BSTAN PA NAM YANG MI NUB
SHOG ,DE NYID 'DZIN PA'I RTZA LAG RNAM 'DREN RJE, ,PHYAG NA
PADMA'I SKU TSE RAB BRTEN CING, ,BSLABS GSUM GTER MDZOD THOS
BSAM NOR BU'I GLING, ,BSHAD SGRUB SDE BZHI'I 'PHRIN LAS RGYAS

PAR SHOG ,'DI'I CHED SGO GSUM NGAL BA BSTAN PA DANG, ,BDAG PA
SPEL SOGS MTHUN RKYAN BSGRUBS PA KUN, ,GNAS SKABS LHA MI'I SRID
PA RIM BRGYUD DE, ,RING MIN SKU GSUM THOB PA'I RGYU RU BSNGO,
,DGE LEGS KUN GYI 'BYUNG GNAS BLA MA DANG, ,DNGOS GRUB 'DZAD MED
GTAR GYUR LHAG PA'I LHA, ,MTHUN

@141A *, ,RKYEN SPEL MDZAD LI BYIN LHA RA CHES, ,BSAM DON LHUN
GRUB BKRA SHIS BDE LEGS MDZOD, ,CES BSTAN BCOS SA CHEN PO MNGOR
PAR RTOGS PA'I RGYAN GYI SPYI DON MKHAS GRUB BSTAN PA DAR RGYAS
KYIS MDZAD PA'I RNAM BSHAD SNYANG PO RGYAN

GYI SNANG BA ZHES BYA BA 'DI SNGA SOR SER SMAD RANG DU PAR ZHIN
YOD PAR SNANG YANG LCAGS SBRUL LA ZHUGS KYIS RKYEN DBANG DU SONG
BA BCAS, SPYI DON GYI BSTAN BCOS 'DI BZHIN BLO GSAL RNAMS LA
PHAN THOGS CHE NGES YOD STABS BSTAN RGYUN LA BSAMS GZHUNG SA NAS
PAR GSAR BSKRUN BGYID RTZIS YOD THOG

RGYAL KHAB PI CING NAS G-YUNG DGON KHRI PA RGYUD STONG SHAR PA
CHAS RJES KYANG BSKUL MA'I NYER LEN LA BRTEN SNGON YOD PAR MA LA
YIG NOR PHRAN BU YOD 'DUG BA RNAMS RANG LUGS KHAS LEN DANG MTHUN
KHYAD SER SMAD THOS BSAM NOR BU'I GLING GI SLOB DPON LAS THOG PA
GRAGS PA 'PHRIN LAS NAS ZHAG 'JUG

BGYIS SHING, DGE BSHES RAB 'BYAMS PA RIN CHEN RGYAL MTSAN DANG,
DKA' BCU 'PHRIN LAS CHOS 'KHOR GNYIS NAS KYANG CHED DU YIG CHAR
DAG THER SKYO SEL LEGS PAR BYAS, DO DAM RTZE DRUNG SPYANG GRONG
BSKAL BZANG 'PHRIN LAS YAR 'PHEL DANG, AE SNYE'I BRIS BRKOS
MKHAS BSDUS

BZHI BCU SKOR NAS ME KHYI LO 'PHAGS PA 'JIG RTEN DBANG PHYUG GI
GZHAL MANG KHANG PHE BRANG CHEN PO PO TA LAR PAR GSAR BSGRUN
BGYIS DUS BAR BYANG SMON TSIG TU SH'AKYA'I DGE SLONG DA MO NO
MON HAN NGAG DBANG 'JAM DPAL BDE LEGS RGYA MTSOS DGA' LDAN
BGSANG SNGAGS DGA' TSAL GYI

GTZUG LAG KHANG DU SBYAR BA 'DIS KYANG RGYAL BA'I BSTAN PA RIN
PO CHE PHYOGS DUS GNAS SKABS THAMS CAD DU DANG ZHING RGYAS LA
YUN RING DU GNAS PA'I RGYUR GYUR CIG, MANGGALAm, ,,
